---------------------------------------------------------
Entries in the above log give the Gedcom Id and sequential Record Number (within record type) of the relevant record.  For example, an entry might start like this:

    Record Type=Individual. Gedcom Id=I34. Record Number=23.

The record's id will match the numeric portion of the Gedcom Id (34 in the example), unless records of that type have been renumbered, in which case, the record id will match the Record Number (23 in the example).  The following record types have been renumbered: Family
